In [191]: 
from collections import defaultdict

def features(text):
    """Convert a post into a dictionary of features"""
    features = defaultdict(int)
    for word in text:
        if word not in nltk.corpus.stopwords.words('english'):
            if word.isalpha():
                features[word.lower()] += 1
    return features

q = backend.QueryBuilder()                    # Create a new custom query
q.set_columns(['Tags'])                       # we are interested specified columns
q.show = False                                # not displaying the result of this query on screen 
q.limit = 0                                   # allows us to take out the result limitations 
mytext = analyzer.get_text( q.execute(con) )  # read the text-body from results 
ALL_TAGS = analyzer.get_most_frequent_words(mytext, 25)  # Print most frequent words 
ALL_TAGS = ALL_TAGS[:5]
######################
train_set = []
for each_tag in ALL_TAGS:
    each_tag = each_tag[0]
    
    q = backend.QueryBuilder()                    # Create a new custom query
    q.set_columns(['Question','Tags'])          # we are interested specified columns
    q.set_condition('Tags', each_tag)
    q.set_condition('AND Question NOT', 'null')       # Question should not be empty
    q.show = False                                # not displaying the result of this query on screen 
    q.limit = 0                                   # allows us to take out the result limitations 
    array_of_questions = q.execute(con)
    print len(array_of_questions)
    whole_text = ''
    
    for item in array_of_questions:
        whole_text+=item[0]
    tokens = nltk.word_tokenize(whole_text)
    train_set.append( (features(tokens), each_tag) )
    
    
c = nltk.FreqDist(item[1] for item in train_set)
default = c.keys()[0]
print default
print c

test_set = []
    
q = backend.QueryBuilder()                    # Create a new custom query
q.set_columns(['Question','Tags'])          # we are interested specified columns
q.set_condition('Question NOT', 'null')       # Question should not be empty
q.set_condition('AND Tags', 'null')
q.show = False                                # not displaying the result of this query on screen 
q.limit = 0                                   # allows us to take out the result limitations 
array_of_questions = q.execute(con)
print len(array_of_questions)

whole_text = ''

for item in array_of_questions:
    whole_text+=item[0]
tokens = nltk.word_tokenize(whole_text)
test_set.append( (features(tokens), 'null') )

q = backend.QueryBuilder()                    # Create a new custom query
q.set_columns(['Question','Tags'])          # we are interested specified columns
q.set_condition('Question NOT', 'null')       # Question should not be empty
q.set_condition('AND Tags', 'null')
q.show = False                                # not displaying the result of this query on screen 
q.limit = 25                                   # allows us to take out the result limitations 
array_of_questions = q.execute(con)

for each in array_of_questions:
    each = each[0]
    print "{0:2.2f}% {1}  {2} ".format( nb.prob_classify(features(nltk.word_tokenize(each))).prob('book')*100, '----', each)
